msg:Overall evaluation: very average, not worth the price.
On the plus side: the hardware is okay.
Poor aspects: the sanitation environment is average, and the cleaning is not careful; there are only western food for self-ordering; there are few types of breakfast and buffet, and they are cold; the service standards are not uniform, and there is a phenomenon of asking for good reviews; There is a helicopter hovering above the hotel, and the sound is so loud that I can't sleep; the sound insulation of the hotel is not good.
I have lived in five-star and super-five-star hotels, but the price is too high compared to my experience, about 1,000 yuan a night is about the same.
